mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年生，宁夏法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始迫害法轮功时，他是一名高校学生，因不放弃信仰，被开除。因不放弃修炼，此前他曾被判刑两次均为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并被拘禁在洗脑班近<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。共曾遭牢狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日高兵又遭盐池县花马池警察抓捕，下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">高兵已遭判刑，被关押在宁夏石嘴山监狱</span>。此次高兵<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被判刑的时间及刑期、关押到监狱的时间等情况均不详</span>。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E7%9B%90%E6%B1%A0%E5%8E%BF%E9%AB%98%E5%85%B5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-431827.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">高方强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">男，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东泰安市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年五十二岁，个体业主。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，谢清玲、高方强等法轮功学员去良庄镇赠送法轮功年历，在回来的路上，警察驾驶围堵抓捕。后泰山区公安分局国保大队与岱庙等派出所撬门破锁，闯入谢清玲家中，将家中所有电脑、打印机、法轮功资料等物品抄走。谢清玲和高方强最后被关押到泰安市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉谢清玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万元；高方强被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。谢清玲和高方强不服，上诉至泰安市中级法院。泰安中院裁定“维持原判”。后谢清玲转入山东省女子监狱服刑；高方强被转入山东省监狱服刑。高方强刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高光成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东潍坊市昌乐县<span lang="EN-US">5</span>图街道办邱家河村法轮功学员。高光成曾在<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份，因修炼法轮功被判刑十年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年出狱。高光成在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，在昌乐县黄埠村讲法轮功时，被黄埠村周涛恶意举报，被昌乐城南派出所抓捕。城南派出所警察高玉柱带领着<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个警察强行抄家。当时因疫情期间各看守所都不收人，高玉柱从高光成手机上找到了他女儿的电话恐吓说，交<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元钱办取保候审手续，不办就送往监狱。他女儿害怕就好说歹说交了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元办理了取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东省潍坊市青州法院对高光成开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高恒：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省黄冈市蕲春县漕河镇上河桥村人，广东省广州市番禺区南浦岛常驻居民，基督徒，广州圣经归正教会信徒，公益人士，中国在押良心犯。因其为人正直，热心公益，笃信基督，经常自觉参与所在教会的各种事工（即服务活动），故经常受到所在教会及区域的民众好评（如<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因广州市再次出现新管病毒升级版疫情，其所在番禺区南浦岛处于封闭管理状态，随百姓生活出现诸多不便，其所在圣经归正教会为此开展了为市民发放生活物资等活动，其一直踊跃参与其中，即是一例）；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因在儿童节当天举牌呼吁“尊重生命”、“反对堕胎”，而令当局不满，次日即被广州市番禺区南浦岛警方强行要求房东对其驱离，后因其及房东持守立场，顶住压力，终未妥协；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，“六四事件”第<span lang="EN-US">32</span>周年受难者纪念日，因其在广州地铁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号线某地铁站举牌“六月四日，为国家祷告”，并将相关图片发于网上，同时在微博上写下：“一切社会层面上的苦难，虽然往往被归结于制度与政治的丑恶，然而，究其根本，它无不源于人心中根深蒂固的罪性。就这一罪性而言，我们与屠杀的决定者、指挥者和执行者，并无根本的不同。感谢主，我们虽同为罪人，却蒙了从上帝而来的奇异恩典，悔改认罪，接受耶稣为主，从而成为上帝的儿女”等心得，很快被广东网警发现告发，遂顿遭广州当局强力打击；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日凌晨，即被广州市番禺区南浦岛派出所警方从家中抓走，自此失联；据悉，其友人称应该已被广州市公安分局警方刑事拘留，涉嫌罪名寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被正式逮捕。高恒于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日不公开开庭审理，未当庭宣判。目前被羁押广州第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/20212022211.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/20212022211.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省东营市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营市东营区胜利派出所、东三路派出所、明月派出所、文汇派出所警察同时出动，商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽等法轮功学员被秘密绑架。商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽被劫持到东营市看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营区法院对商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽庭审，并判处：王子明<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，商兆香<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；张爱丽<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元。四人上诉到东营市中级法院中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。高洪伟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员李嘉惠、张盛全、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美被抓捕，两年多后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才获悉已经被判刑。高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。高洪伟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市绥中县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，绥中县国保大队副大队长刘唤宇等人，闯到高华家，抓捕了高华和高英姐妹，以及去串门的法轮功学员陈文艳和王彦东，抢劫了高华家的电脑、打印机等私人财物。高华被关押在葫芦岛看守所，高英被关押在葫芦岛拘留所，王彦东被关押在绥中看守所。陈文艳被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高华、高英、王彦东被构陷到绥中县检察院。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，高英回家，被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，高华、王彦东被构陷案到了葫芦岛连山检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日高华、王彦东被葫芦岛市连山法院判刑：高华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，王彦东<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；高华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E9%AB%98%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E7%8E%8B%E5%BD%A6%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434280.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高惠仙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日生，原云南省昆明钢铁公司桥钢厂职工，后被非法开除公职。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续迫害中，高惠仙曾两次被中共判刑，共遭冤狱九年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日高惠仙向安宁市太平街道办事处龙箐村中共支部书记何顺贵讲法轮功真相，同时赠送了一本「明慧日历」向他祝福。结果何顺贵向公安机关诬告高惠仙。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日高惠仙正在母亲家里，被安宁市国保大队警察非法撬锁入室抓捕、抄家，警察抢走计算机、打印机、大法书籍、法轮功数据等大量私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被昆明市西山区法院判刑七年，罚款一千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高继萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高建君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高建君被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高金平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，保定市依棉厂退休职工，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>中午，高金平在保定市满城区出租房内被保定市公安局国保警察和保定市竞秀区依棉派出所抓捕，并同时抢走电脑、大法书籍等个人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，高阳县法院对高金平开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，高金平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">高菊芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西新余市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，高菊芳到一小区发法轮功资料，被人举报，随后被警察抄家，家里的法像和法轮功书籍全部抄走，被关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月得知，高菊芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/1/31/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-419315.html#2113022538-1"><b 11.0pt;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，高俊、张永宝二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高立娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津石化公司青年女教师、法轮功学员。高立娟<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被当地警察绑架。高立娟遭构陷的案卷两次被检察院退回，办案单位大港胜利派出所及大港国继续罗列罪名，又把高立娟起诉到天津滨海新区法院，意欲高立娟重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日高立娟案在天津滨海新区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万。高丽娟上诉被驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; 106%;">山东省临沂市兰山区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。一九九九年七月江泽民发动对法轮功的迫害之后，高西霞被迫离家在外。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，高西霞到兰山区北园路纽约上城发放真相资料时，被不明真相的人举报，随后被育才路派出所抓捕，第二天她取保候审回到家中。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，派出所和国保以不配合签字为由，在没有搜查证和拘留证的情况下派出所警察及国保人员强行撬她家的门锁，把人带走，并将她家里的银行卡及现金翻走。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，兰山区法院进行了庭审，期间以家属是证人为由，阻止家属旁听，并阻止家属申请亲友辩护，不允许家属为高西霞辩护。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，兰山区法院对高西霞判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：高晓歧被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金两万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html</span></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高小娓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，农民，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆（洗脑班）至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被铐在铁椅子上<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天，臀部都坐烂了，后被关押在宝鸡市第二看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，宝鸡市金台区法院给下达起诉书及监视居住六个月通知。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高小雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北保定市易县裴山镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，易县城区派出所副所长靖明忠和警察刘国栋两人，跨省前往贵州省遵义市，在高小雄的打工单位，突然对他实施抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被河北涿州市法院刑庭在易县法庭通过视频庭审。近日，易县看守所打电话给高小雄的父母：高小雄被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">高永丽</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江穆棱市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，穆棱市建行小区的一位老人曹淑芳家中的玻璃碎了，法轮功学员孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人帮其修理。国保警察突然出现抓捕了孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人，并抄了三人的家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，海林市法院下判决，高永丽被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，高朋光和孙士伟被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处以两万罚金。高永丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高智晟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，陕西省榆林市佳县人，著名维权律师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起，开始替弱势群体维权打官司，曾处理过多宗民间维权案件；自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底起，开始多次上书中共当局高层，要求改变对法轮功等群体的非法处理手段，并参与对法轮功学员器官遭当局活摘指控的调查；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，与妻子公开宣布退出中国共产党；因其勇于于为当局认定的敏感性案件（注：含法轮功信仰者、地下基督教徒以及与官员发生纠纷的底层农民和私营企业家）辩护，故而曾多次受到中共官方机构或组织（<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室）黑社会手段的严重骚扰和打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其执业执照被当局吊销，随后被秘密绑架并遭到约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日起其与外界失联，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月才被当局释放返京；后因其接受了美联社采访，遂被再次与外界失联，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其亲友才从新华社报导中得知，其缓刑已被北京法院撤销，须继续服刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日刑满出狱，此前在新疆维吾尔自治区沙雅监狱服刑。出狱后高智晟仍被严密监控，且不让治牙看病，致其因长期在狱中遭受酷刑折磨和被单独囚禁，迄今仍牙齿松动，身体健康欠佳；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在陕北老家秘密撰写的新书《<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，起来中国》在台湾正式印刷出售，因该书涉及中共当局对其长期绑架、囚禁和施以酷刑等，以及他从信仰角度看中共<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年将会灭亡和对<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年后的中国未来宪政民主化展望等三大内容，遂令当局十分恐惧、恼怒，对其监控愈加严密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬在老家失踪，后获知被当局控制带回北京关押。目前已遭强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年多，音信全无，生死不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京市丰台区岳各庄的维权残疾人。住北京丰台区魏家村南<span lang="EN-US">20</span>号院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号楼门<span lang="EN-US">2</span>门<span lang="EN-US">1305</span>室。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，葛志慧和同区石榴庄东街<span lang="EN-US">195</span>号的被强拆人李美青，到达中央扫黑除恶督导组驻地反映政府的黑社会化强拆，结果在督导组驻地的门口，遭到丰台区副区长带队的维稳人员的阻截，求见扫黑除恶督导组未果。但是，没隔多久，葛志慧竟遭刑事拘留。罪名是寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，葛志慧被构陷案开庭，未当庭宣判。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后葛志慧涉寻衅滋事一案于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，在北京市丰台区法院通过视频方式宣判，葛志慧被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现被关押在丰台看守所。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">格桑梅朵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨一小学女教师。格桑梅朵是第一位可以被知道的因翻墙而遭中共当局强迫失踪的藏人。据了解，格桑梅朵曾在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>上转发外媒 《自由亚洲电台》和《挪威西藏之声》中文部有关藏区的新闻报道，以促进使用<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>的中国网友，特别是她的汉族朋友们了解西藏问题的真相。梅朵非常了解西藏的历史和现实。格桑梅朵翻墙转发外媒西藏新闻一事被发现后，当局开始对她进行迫害，她所在的小学将梅朵开除，梅朵继而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年遭到当局强迫失踪，至今已下落不明<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现获悉，格桑梅朵被以“泄露国家秘密”定罪，关押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">格桑秀郎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达木寺僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后一直被秘密关押，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被拉萨市中级法院以“带领民众集会”罪名判处<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑。目前被关押在西藏拉萨的扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革命（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">他与叶尔波里（哈萨克）都是新疆伊犁州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县哈萨克族人，自由职业者，伊斯兰教信仰者，哈萨克族人权捍卫者。由于没有办理信教许可证（即未到当地政府部门申请批准），坚持自行做祷告，并经常到清真寺，因此于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月被抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬分别被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。据一位哈萨克同乡称，因他们都无正式职业，平时靠打散工或装修房子度日，二人家庭都十分贫困。被捕后，当地公安不准家属聘请律师，也拒绝向家属出示判决书。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革振华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">63</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区人，原阿城区低压电器厂职工，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年曾被哈尔滨市阿城市公安局非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。在哈尔滨市长林子劳教所期间，经常遭到警察和犯人的毒打，被强迫长时间坐小板凳等。因劳教所环境恶劣，他身上长满了疥疮，疼痛难忍。每天还要强迫他做十几个小时的苦役，完不成任务就罚站。其左肋骨曾被警察和犯人打断两根，但仍不放过他，逼他出工干活，一天也不许休息。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日凌晨，他在哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被当地警方闻讯赶来围捕、绑架，后被关押在尚志市看守所。与其一起的法轮功学员菽坤和王翠娥也遭抓捕，至今未归。因长期不知革振华的消息，其妻经多方打听，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才知道丈夫革振华已被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。据悉，革振华不服，提起上诉，但二审仍维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。目前服刑地不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根敦伦珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，青海藏族作家、诗人，曾是青海同仁县隆务寺僧人，过去曾数次被当局逮捕。同仁县熟悉此事的消息人士介绍，根敦伦珠对保护母语藏语文和西藏文化非常关心。他的作品在境内和流亡藏人拥有很大的影响力。根敦伦珠于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年十月在网站上发表了一首诗歌，内容是作家和艺术家需要有言论和思想不受限制的自由。尽管面临诸多限制，根敦伦珠仍坚持创作，并从其读者处获得支持。青海当局制订的藏区“扫黑除恶”政策中，把提倡“保护母语”视为黑恶势力行为。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，青海省黄南州藏族作家、诗人根敦伦珠被中共当局逮捕，关押至秘密地点，下落不明。据悉，当局在对其实施长时间监视后采取了这个行动。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根托（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根托，现年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根珠，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">耿福霞<span lang="EN-US">:<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、尉国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。当时被抓捕的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员被构陷到遵化市法院。河北唐山市遵化法院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日对<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、尉国申、付瑞英、陆彩云开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日判耿福霞<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿家峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，山东省沂水县籍人，山东省淄博市桓台县马桥镇辛庄村村民，维权访民，实名举报人，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，就开始因所在村落官员严重贪腐问题而实名举报维权，随被山东省桓台县当局视为需要打压的异己和维稳对象；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因先后三次上访投诉，被恒台县警方以“非正常上访”为由给予严厉警告；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，曾两次被恒台县警方以“非正常上访，扰乱公共场所秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，又被以警方“故意损害财物”、“扬言实施放火，非法携带管制刀具”为由分别处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因所在辛庄村村主任郭世勋从金城石化公司往辛庄村的西北角运输化工废渣，污染土地，而向山东省各级环保部门举报，无果后，又于次日欲往北京环保部举报，随被县政府派人拦截并遭人毒打住院；过后其虽多次继续举报违法排污的村主任郭世勋，并要求警方尽快查处打人事件和为其被殴打导致常年半头痛后遗症做鉴定，但都被拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其再次被恒台县警方抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并被要求退赔相关经济损失<span lang="EN-US">2803</span>元。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因桓台县田庄镇文庄村的维权人士张岗遭抓捕，张岗之妹向其求助，其为营救张岗，遂不惧险境，多次向各级主管部门及新闻媒体举报、控诉恒台县公安局非法拘禁人，从而引社会热议；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因维权者张岗已被批捕，其受张岗妹妹之托，立刻在微信群频繁发“紧急关注”，以呼吁更多正义人士关注张岗被捕事件；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，再次为声援张岗被抓事件而在新浪微博网站发文，揭露张岗所在田庄镇文庄村村委主任组织黑社会，贪污受贿、公账私存、挪用公款等渎职行为，因此文被人关注、转发近千次，遂立遭恒台县当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被恒台县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等再次刑拘，随后又被恒台县检察院很快以多项罪由正式批捕，并关押于桓台县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被淄博市恒台县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月）、“妨碍公务罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月）、“敲诈勒索罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月）三罪，数罪并罚决定执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被山东省淄博市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US"> 2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前疑似在山东省淄博监狱（又称山东省第四监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿录堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东东营法轮功学员。耿录堂、邹佩霞老夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已年过七旬，家住东营市胜利油田孤岛采油厂芙蓉小区。修炼大法前，夫妻俩身体很不好，耿录堂还患有高血压等疾病。一九九六年前后，老俩口修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，老俩口去河口地区赶集，向人宣传法轮功，遭人恶告，东营市河口区国保大队下属的义和镇派出所警察，于当天抓捕了夫妇俩。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后耿录堂、邹佩霞夫妇均被东营市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被勒索罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52140367"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿潇男：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52140367;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年代出生，出版人，独立电视制作人，文化企业家，传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司董事长，北京文化公共领域领军人物，公益文化思想活动策划<span lang="EN-US">/</span>执行<span lang="EN-US">/</span>传播者，中国在押政治犯。 耿潇男早年曾就读于中央戏剧学院，毕业后逐渐成为中国文化出版人，电影人，历任中国天画画天影业首席执行官、瑞雅书业总编辑，之后又和丈夫秦真共同创立传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司，并担任董事长，随在业界知名度较高；近年来，因在北京文化公共领域以活跃、敢言着称，并积极致力于公益文化思想活动策划、执行及传播活动等，遂遭北京当局的维稳监控打压；<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦真<span lang="EN-US">/</span>耿潇男夫妇二人突然被警方带走，随后被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌”非法经营罪“刑拘，现在北京市海淀区看守所关押；北京当局曾以经济问题为名调查其二人所属的出版公司，其丈夫与公司的账号均被查封；多名好友均称其被抓捕，恐与此前公开为多名中国公共知识分子及异见人士发声呼吁有关，乃是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月遭正式逮捕。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日遭中共当局抓捕的著名媒体人耿潇男女士因言获罪被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。后上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日二审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日由北京市海淀区看守所转北京女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耿宜敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇环北七路<span lang="EN-US">47</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂会堂主任，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，该基督教会接到当地县政府发来的欲拆除教会通知，声称政府要对阜南县富陂大道西侧实施棚改项目，而其教堂因位于该项目征收范围，所以需要拆除；因政府仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称若要异地重建政府将不予相应补偿，面对此单方武断决策，其及牧师、众信徒们认为明显有失公允，故遭到包括其在教会众教友的坚决反对，遂遭当局恶意报复与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，当教堂众教友在做礼拜聚会时，突遭地方当局的强行闯入拆除，拆除时无任何合法文件及通知出示，且因事发突然，教堂财物来不及搬出，以致所有物品近都毁坏；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与教会牧师、部分会堂成员数人被阜南县警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原审，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿则军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区磐石教会传道。宁夏回族自治区石嘴山市惠农区磐石教会于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午两点半左右，在惠农区水厂一处比较偏僻的平房聚会的过程中，被石嘴山市惠农区公安分局国保和各派出所民警，宗教局冲击。在场的老年人登记后被送回住处，其他人一律带走问话。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>号，教会的传道耿则军以扰乱社会秩序被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，他妻子还有其他四位基督徒则被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">8:30</span>耿则军又被叫去问话，晚上家人打电话才知道耿则军又以涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集被刑事拘留，并在<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日以组织非法聚集罪批捕，现羁押在石嘴山市看守所，先前被行政拘留的其他五人则以同样罪名被取保候审。耿则军于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/2022125.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/2022125.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宫文义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了宫文义等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其他<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名法轮功学员被松北区检察院起诉。宫文义因身体原因保外回家，检察院称另案处理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，宫文义在哈尔滨市江北住处，警察再次抓捕，并被抄家。后被在哈市第一看守所关押。后宫文义于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被哈市道外区法院秘密开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被押送哈市呼兰监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">巩进军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曾因房屋遭遇强拆而上访多年，并屡遭截访，被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因长期滞留北京上访，遂被送至黑监狱马家楼关押，后又被遣返原籍，途中其一行四人（均为访民）因遭到黑保安的非人虐待且拘不让饮食，故而在其人身自由及安全被“黑保安”非法严重侵害的情况下被迫予以正当防卫，双方发生激烈冲突，引发刺死黑保安事件（警方称一死一伤）；案发后河北省饶阳县警方迅速将其抓捕刑拘，并被关押在河北省衡水市深州看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被河北省衡水市中院以“故意伤害罪”判处无期徒刑；据悉其在被审讯时曾遭严重酷刑，仅一天即被电击<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次。目前在河北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡嘎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡藏民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早从<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，中国政府就开始计划将在拉萨市林周县附近的矿区建设、实施“旁多水利枢纽工程”。因该工程要在两条交汇于林周县旁多乡的河流——热振河、旁多措河之上筑坝截水，故为确保顺利开工，相关政府部门就于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召开藏民大会，郑告村民此工程是“中共中央的指令，若有藏人试图阻止施工，将以政治罪名进行拘捕”。随后几年，因有关部门迅速投入大量施工准备，不仅在当地做频繁测量、建桥及建路等工作，而且炸山挖石，大量采矿，随意排放污水，导致当地的自然生态环境出现严重毁坏，附近村民的民房出现裂痕及大面积农田被毁坏等现象。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因拉萨市林周县的“旁多水利枢纽工程”正式开工，当局随立即强迫旁多乡<span lang="EN-US">119</span>户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>名）藏民尽快整体搬迁。因当地藏民不愿搬迁，故而多次向政府部门提出投诉请求，但均毫无果效。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，遂被迫进行集体维权与和平请愿，以期能借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目。不料却遭到中共西藏当局的强烈打压。贡嘎、白玛等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名藏族人权捍卫者因此遭拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，贡嘎、白玛等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案分别被拉萨市法院以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由秘判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等徒刑，其亦被判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡觉尼玛（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州（以下简称阿坝州）若尔盖县人，西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺果芒学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期进入西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺的果芒学院对佛教进修、研读；后因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成其身边主要弟子，加之自身对佛学严谨博学的治学态度，故而被哲蚌寺果芒学院确立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因藏区发生大规模以僧侣为主体，要求中共当局实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁让达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求的抗议活动，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在寺庙约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧人亦积极参与其中，致使抗议活动态势迅速扩展到整个拉萨市区，以及四川、青海等藏区；针对此次抗议游行，中共西藏当局很快调拨大批持枪武警，因管控手段过于极端，遂导致双方发生对峙冲突，其间有不少僧人被抓捕，其余人等被送回寺庙严管看守；尽管此前其并未参加抗议游行活动，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“抗议活动”抓走刑拘，自此失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后其被拉萨市检察院正式批捕，理由是未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，其狱中具体境况等信息不明。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡却卓玛（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因手中举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，在县城一处街道上和平游行，以此表达自己对达赖喇嘛尊者的崇敬，随立即被驻守在街道附近的中共警方拘捕。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">龚月贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，家住武穴市刊江办事处，目前被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。龚月贵刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苟正琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。苟正琼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龚鲭林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市仪陇县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，仪陇县金城镇派出所警察打电话给龚鲭林，让他把身份证拿去派出所登记一下。龚鲭林就拿着自己的身份证，去当地派出所登记，结果被警察抓捕。警察从龚鲭林身上强行搜去他家的钥匙，去他家抄家，警察非法抄走的龚鲭林的私人财物有：法轮功书籍、计算机、打印机等，现金八万多元。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，龚鲭林被庭审，并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">龚圣亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督教牧师，华南教案首犯。龚圣亮牧师是湖北省枣阳市人，华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）的创始人和领袖，该教派是中国一个家庭教会团契，在几个省份有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名信徒。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，龚圣亮在湖北省钟祥市被捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，他被湖北省荆门市中级法院裁定罪名成立，根据中国的反邪教法判处死刑。但由于国际压力，中国放弃了宗教罪名和死刑，并下令重新审判。中国湖北省高级法院后以事实不清、证据不足为由驳回了荆门市中级法院对基督教华南教会五名成员的死刑判决后，荆门市中级法院重新作出一审判决，把龚圣亮、徐福明、胡勇等三人改判无期徒刑，龚邦坤、李英改判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，原先在一审被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年徒刑的向凤屏和刘先知等四人获当庭释放。一些作证反对龚的人后来表示，他们遭到了残酷的刑讯逼供。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区人，原任职乌鲁木齐政府机关工作人员，网络作家，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件发生时用手机短信向境外担任挪威维吾尔协会副秘书长的丈夫拜合提亚尔联系<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多次通报看到的情况，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被新疆乌鲁木齐市警方逮捕，据称在拘留期间曾遭受酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威”罪判处无期徒刑。此前曾在乌鲁木齐水磨沟女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年中共新疆当局录制的认罪悔过视频中，因曾签署了一份书面忏悔声明，遂其刑期被减为<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；但因无法确认具体减刑日期，故其服刑到期日，暂不明晰；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前在乌鲁木齐市新疆第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_99.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_99.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">古丽仙•阿巴斯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔族，退休医生，在押中国政治犯。被捕入狱前，为人生性善良、无私、正直，虽不热衷于参与政治，但有积极的奉献精神；自中共当局对新疆地区各少数族群（尤其是维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族人等）实行更严厉的高压管控以来，因其曾公开批评中共当局针对新疆维吾尔族等族群的人权不尊重、很糟糕，遂遭致新疆中共当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被新疆警方带走，自此失联；后经长达两年多的家人及国际人权组织机构连手查寻，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日终于获悉，其早被当地检察院以多项罪由予以批捕，指控其因“参与恐怖组织”、“恐怖活动”，其行为已严重地扰乱了社会秩序，故被抓捕、判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，被新疆维吾尔自治区某法院以“恐怖组织罪”、“说明恐怖活动罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷明龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北保定市定州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，谷明龙因到高蓬镇钮店村发放法轮功资料被定州市公安局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底被定州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在唐山某监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">顾超：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江苏省南京市溧水区法轮功学员。顾超<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年开始修炼大法。她在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日讲真相时，被人诬告，被溧水区阳镇派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被南京市雨花区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E6%B1%9F%E8%8B%8F%E7%9C%81%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%AC%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%A1%BE%E8%B6%85%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441615.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/23/%E6%B1%9F%E8%8B%8F%E7%9C%81%E5%8D%97%E4%BA%AC%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%A1%BE%E8%B6%85%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441615.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">关兴涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日关兴涛与妻子吴艳华被抓捕、构陷，后被大庆市让胡路区法院判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。妻子吴艳华被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害。关兴涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-421367.html#2122522533-1"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:
