style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾国玺：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，原籍甘肃会宁人，成都电子科技大学毕业以后在广东深圳外贸工作和安家，后以写电脑软件为生。与各地民运人士多有往来，行事低调，很少有人知道他的情况。曾联署过《零八宪章》和多个人权呼吁书。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日贾国玺遭山东省阳谷县公安局刑事拘留，罪名是“颠覆国家政权”。目前被羁押在阳谷县看守所。截至目前，其亲属知晓与否、律师是否已有介入等均情况不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贾乃芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生。贾乃芝一九九七年十一月开始修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月二十日中共江泽民集团开始疯狂迫害法轮功，二十多年来，贾乃芝遭受的残酷迫害数不胜数，多次被抓捕，被羁押在拘留所、自强学校、教养院、看守所、监狱，长时间过着暗无天日的生活，多种酷刑迫害，身心受到严酷的摧残，累计冤狱十多年，自由被剥夺，财产被抢去，受邪恶政策株连，善良的丈夫承受不住压力被迫离婚，年迈的母亲长期思念女儿不得见，含泪而死，孩子得不到妈妈的照顾，遭遇二十多年的迫害，使贾乃芝夫离子散，家破人亡。贾乃芝<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被抓捕，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被关押到辽宁女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月期间检查出肝病大三阳（传染期）。贾乃芝的家属给辽宁女子监狱狱警打了电话，了解一下贾乃芝的身体情况，监狱并没有给贾乃芝医治，家属要求保外就医，监狱狱警说，办不了。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贾淑娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃省白银市会宁县郭城镇法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出生，家住会宁县郭城驿镇红堡村<span lang="EN-US">1</span>社<span lang="EN-US">95</span>号，农民。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年后，贾淑娟遭到中共当局包括抓捕、关押、劳教、判刑的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，会宁县公安局国保大队在外面抓捕了贾淑娟夫妇。现得知，她已被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前被关押在甘肃省兰州市位于九州开发区的女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/19/%E4%B9%B0%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E5%A6%92%E5%AB%89-%E7%94%98%E8%82%83%E5%86%9C%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441469.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/19/%E4%B9%B0%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E5%A6%92%E5%AB%89-%E7%94%98%E8%82%83%E5%86%9C%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441469.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">嘉扬多吉（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，是甘孜县色西底乡木西村人，遭捕前以放牧为生。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14&nbsp;</span>日独自在县城一条街道上开展了和平示威活动，声喊出“允许达赖喇嘛尊者返回西藏”、“西藏要自由”等口号，抗议中共的治藏政策，随即遭到公安拘捕。当局稍后要求嘉扬多吉的亲友们，前往甘孜县公安局登记电话和手机号码，并警告他们不得将此消息传出境外。后信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">嘉央洛追（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县人，阿坝县甲尔多乡孜郎寺僧人嘉央洛追，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年约<span lang="EN-US">35</span>岁。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜晚在马尔康县人民医院门前被当局拘捕。据信僧人嘉央洛追是因为在微信上撰写并发送涉及“敏感”内容的文章，而被中共政府拘捕。后信息全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">加尔肯别克·卡生巴依（哈）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆维吾尔自治区博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市人，哈萨克族，职业不详，哈萨克国移民，宗教人士，中国在押良心犯。已于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年退休，之前曾多次前往哈萨克国（以下简称哈国）；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，正式移民至哈萨克国；因协助其妻及其两名孩子也移民到哈国，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，从哈国返回中国时，被新疆博乐市当局以“传播宗教极端思想，鼓励新疆哈萨克族人移民哈萨克”为由送入“去极端化培训中心”羁押；后虽有暂短释放，但很快又于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博乐市警方收监逮捕；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市法院以“煽动民族仇恨，民族分裂罪”、“宗教极端犯罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月</b>；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其逃往国外的儿子珠玛丹<span lang="EN-US">.</span>加尔肯别克因不堪父亲蒙冤入狱被判，被迫向哈萨克国总统、外交部及社会菁英们发出求助呼吁，以期能使其父尽快获救；另据悉，截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其家人尚未收到任何官方对其的刑事裁决通知书；其妻、女因此受牵连，妻子图尔逊古丽<span lang="EN-US">.</span>努尔海已于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被原退休单位博乐市达勒特镇中心小学停发退休金，女儿山山古丽<span lang="EN-US">.</span>加尔肯因帮其聘请、委托辩护律师，亦被送入“去极端化培训中心”羁押，至今失联。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">江莲花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">江西省南昌市南昌县莲塘镇法轮功学员，女。江莲花因派发法轮功资料遭人举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在莲塘家中被警察抓捕。后她被关押在莲塘看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，江莲花被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。据悉，警察欲于年后将她转到江西女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江增朝：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，又名江曾潮，黑龙江省绥化市青冈县人，绥化市安达市常居公民，个体小商户，法轮功信仰者，自由信仰权利捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始接受并信仰法轮功；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，曾因时任中共最高领导人江泽民开始打压迫害法轮功，为捍卫自由信仰权利，随进京上访被遣回，并被黑龙江省安达市警方非法关进看守所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天，惨遭酷刑折磨和毒打，并被戴死刑犯使用的沉重脚镣，后又被青冈县警方继续关押<span lang="EN-US">21</span>天才被释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又被安达市朝阳派出所警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，并送安达市看守所关押<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因坚持锻炼法轮功而被绥化市当局处以劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，且被关在黑龙江省绥化劳教所服劳役；获释后，为生计，且为躲避当局打压和避免家人受牵连，而曾被迫在辽宁省盘锦市靠打工为生；然因其一边打工一边仍不忘进行法轮功宣传，于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被辽宁省盘锦市警方野蛮拘捕；后其案件被移交到辽宁省盘锦市法院，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被该法院一审以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并被先送到辽宁省沈阳第二监狱（大北监狱）创二监区服刑，后又转送到大连南关岭监狱（大连市第一监狱）接续服刑；刑满出狱后，其为生计被迫又到黑龙江省大庆市谋生；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，再次因散发、宣传法轮功数据，故而与其妹江洪艳一同被大庆市让胡路区龙南派出所警方以涉嫌“宣传邪教罪”从家中抓走、刑拘，且被分别关押在大庆市林甸县看守所和太康县看守所；后其妹被取保释放，而其仍被继续羁押并被让胡路区检察院以同罪由予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其案在黑龙江省大庆市让胡路区法院开庭审理，终被该法院一审以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉；后经大庆市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱（黑龙江省哈尔滨市呼兰区腰堡乡<span lang="EN-US">803</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">150521</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">姜凤丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁凤城市宝山镇法轮功学员。姜凤丽于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被抓捕，据家属说是丹东市公安局直接来抓人、抄家，清早去的，当时姜凤丽还没起床。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月家属得到消息，姜凤丽已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被关押在辽宁女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">姜奎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，基督徒，黔东南州凯里市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，教会聚会点骨干成员及带领人（之一），中国在押良心犯。自从参与贵州省凯里市基督复临安息日教会聚会点的敬拜活动以来，因一直致力于热忱服务教会的多种事工活动，随深得教会聚会点长老与众信徒的信任和赞许；但因该教会聚会点<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年来一直属于家庭教会聚会模式，对中共当局严格把控的“三自教会”管理拒不认同也不接受，虽然早已向贵州省宗教局提交请求教会聚会点合法的申请，但却始终未获审批，故遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛限制；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因该聚会点信徒不断增多，聚会点迅速由原先的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个增加到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个，遂引起贵州省黔东南州当局的注意与恐慌，并迅速成立项目组，对其聚会点进行全面侦查；之后，其及教会长老等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位神职人员悉数被黔东南州凯里市警方带走，并被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联；后其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人又被黔东南州凯里市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，控其因聚会点申请未被国家审批，众信徒所交奉献款均属于诈骗款，故其一切教会行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案被黔东南州凯里市法院一审分别以“诈骗罪”枉法判处<span lang="EN-US">12</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其中，姜奎被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；其不服判决，已向黔东南州中级法院提起上诉；二审正在等待中。目前姜奎被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">姜淑波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，辽宁瓦房店市复州城镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，张宝玲、姜淑波与慈美云三名老年女法轮功学员，去讲三台乡讲清法轮功被迫害真相，被辽宁省大连市三台乡派出所抓捕、关押、抄家。随后送瓦房店看守所隔离关押半个月后，羁押在大连姚家看守所。后被批捕。张宝玲、姜淑波、慈美云于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日开庭。后张宝玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，姜淑波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜淑娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省莱西法轮功学员。原是山东省莱西市汽车站职工，她因坚持对法轮功的信仰被开除公职及遭受多种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日姜淑娥在做家政的户主楼下遭莱西国保李为魁等人绑架，关押在普东看守所，后被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姜淑梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，沈阳市皇姑区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。在中共对法轮功持续至今<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的迫害中，姜淑梅曾被劳教、判刑，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，姜淑梅被关押在辽宁马三家教养院迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年后，被关押辽宁省女子监狱迫害。累计被关押迫害<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，皇姑区公安分局新乐派出所<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个警察，闯到姜淑梅的家中，抓捕了姜淑梅，并抢走了大法书籍、电脑、打印机等私人物品。姜淑梅被秘密关押到沈阳市看守所。后获悉姜淑梅又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/29/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E6%B2%88%E9%98%B3%E5%A7%9C%E6%B7%91%E6%A2%85%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-434164.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/29/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E6%B2%88%E9%98%B3%E5%A7%9C%E6%B7%91%E6%A2%85%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-434164.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">姜伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省朝阳市法轮功女学员。姜伟因为坚持真善忍信仰，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被非法劳教三年；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被非法判刑八年；期间她被迫离婚、遭受酷刑，被关精神病院，被摧残得了胃癌。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，姜伟再次遭绑架，半年后又被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">姜文忠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">烟台退役军人。烟台海阳市发城镇中夏屋庄村农民。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年因烟台交警违规执法，姜文忠被交警的车撞伤，医生说最低将造成九级伤残。为讨回公道，姜文忠向有关部门控告烟台交警，烟台交警最后同意赔偿<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万，向姜文忠支付了<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万，另<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万转给了发城镇政府。为了讨回这<span lang="EN-US">15</span>万，姜文忠继续控告烟台交警，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底姜文忠到北京后，被海阳截访人员强行带回，从此失去自由。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底被以寻衅滋事罪刑拘，随后被逮捕，初被羁押在海阳看守所，后被转至烟台市看守所。在烟台市看守所羁押至今期间被同室羁押人员殴打过几十次，他曾绝食四天多以示抗争，现虽然已被调换监室，但被殴打的问题依然没有彻底解决，会见时他告诉律师，调换监室后现在开始遭受辱骂，随时可能被打。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_17.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_17.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姜野飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川成都人，约生于<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年，民主人士，人权捍卫者，参加过“八九”学运，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年“汶川地震”后又积极参与维权活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年“六四”前夕，姜野飞在曼谷中共国大使馆门前参与纪念“六四”二十周年静坐活动，被泰国当局抓捕，关押近三年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日与董广平逃亡泰国，二人同被泰国警方在其持有联合国难民署签发的“庇护申请者证明书”（实为保护信）的前提下又以涉嫌“偷渡罪”抓捕，并关押于泰国曼谷市沙吞移民监狱；后经各方民主人士努力和紧急呼吁，被联合国难民署获悉，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日答应拟启动紧急通道，力促使其全家获准难民身份；但<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日仍被中共当局以“非法越境罪”遣送押解回国。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被重庆公安局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”、“组织他人偷越国境罪”逮捕。目前羁押于重庆市第二看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，重庆市第一中级法院对姜野飞颠覆国家政权、偷越国境案宣判，认定姜野飞犯颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，犯偷越国境罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金一千元（人民币，下同），决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金一千元。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜志林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆博乐市访民姜志林下肢残疾，在博乐市务农。因自治区水利厅新水饮《<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>》<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号文件不落实，造成村民长期用水困难。姜志林为此逐级上访反映，均不但得不到解决，反而多次遭到威胁、殴打、拘留。之前姜志林因为举报村主任贪腐，被警方一再迫害打击，拘留多次，上访拦截抓捕，当地政府一直企图把姜志林构陷入狱。姜志林热心公益，经常以 “南国林子”的网名转发微博。他身残志坚，曾在小安妮失学事件中，大力呼吁网民关注，还不断为入狱的郭飞雄等良心犯呼吁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月据知情者透露：姜志林曾签字接受了当地有关基层部门每月一千五百元低保待遇，却被以“敲诈勒索罪”遭当地检察院批捕。姜志林是<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆博乐警方抓捕的，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被当地检察院以“敲诈勒索罪”逮捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，新疆博乐姜志林母亲周女士介绍：“正在新疆伊犁新源县哈拉布拉监狱服刑的姜志林，身体虚弱目光呆滞。除了体重明显下降外，目前已经不能正常说话。狱方说是患有脑梗正在接受治疗之中。”姜母想了解更多有关生情况，却被工作人员粗暴拒绝。具体刑期不明。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案在新疆博乐市法院秘密庭审，终被一审以“敲诈勒索罪”、“诬陷罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；二审维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月传出其已病危。</b>目前在新疆哈拉布拉监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源县哈拉布拉镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835814</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蒋凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北保定市安国市法轮功学员。蒋凤<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被国保大队副队长陈彦青等抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被偷偷开庭、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蒋湛春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省镇江市京口区的维权人士。因为在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年清明时到北京福田公墓祭奠杨佳，在“十一”维稳时，被公安以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”指定监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年的最后一天，蒋湛春被第二次指定居所监视居住，被延长监视居住。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年清明节前夕<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日律师会见了蒋湛春，已经接到了起诉书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日已开庭。仍未判决。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">又据悉，因其在监视居住期间曾屡遭毒打，以致双腿站无法站立，与律师会见时只能用膝盖艰难走路；又因多次被打，难以忍受，曾用网线自杀和割腕自杀；律师与其会见时，见其手上缝有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>针疤痕。目前被羁押于江苏省镇江市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/36_17.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/36_17.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">焦孟娇<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，焦孟娇等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括焦孟娇在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。焦孟娇被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19</span></b></a></span><b class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">焦其华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：焦其华被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">金丽燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，福建省宁德市法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，金丽燕与肖传雄、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、庄友布、陈开奇、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月其被取保候审，后因其继续从事法轮功宣传活动，又被收监逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，金丽燕被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省七台河市法轮功修炼人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初因去哈尔滨看望同修家孩子（同修因依兰县国保半夜上家砸门从窗户跳落时绳索断裂至死）时，在校门口被埋伏的依兰县国保抓走，现行政拘留后刑事拘留。期间律师一直未获得会见。当时律师向住所检察室反应情况，检察院住所检察室主人也配合看守所撒谎说人不在看守所了，也不告知人是释放了还是被哪个办案机关转移走了。因为疫情原因，案子<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号经过检察院两次退补后送到了法院。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月金玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">靳玉玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河南省信阳市浉河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日法轮功学员白玉珍、靳玉玲被信阳市警察入室抓捕，后被构陷至信阳市潢川县检察院、法院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在看守所遭开庭。靳玉玲<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁；白玉珍老人<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，进法庭时，身体走路都不稳。在开庭过程中，靳玉玲、白玉珍一直还被强制戴着手铐。靳玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；白玉珍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。靳玉玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">景春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，吉林省盘石市人，吉林省盘石市安乐乡村民，维权冤民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因与同村另一村民发生的一次冲突而被警方于次年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日刑拘，并关押在盘石市公安局东山看守所，遭受严刑拷打；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被当地法院利用虚假证据，在未开庭的情况下，以“故意伤害罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，赔偿伤害人医药费<span lang="EN-US">1711.97</span>元；后经其妻刘金艳多次维权上诉，法院才不得不改判其无罪，并于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日将其释放；获释后，因其就被枉法关押一年一案依法向法院提出国家赔偿申请，遭到法院无理拒绝，遂被迫走上漫长艰辛的维权之路，期间多次遭遇到地方当局的打击与迫害，身心俱损；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年底，因其再次向当地政府提出信访诉求，随被 盘石市警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日强行抓捕，并以涉嫌“敲诈勒索（政府）罪”被刑拘，关押于吉林省盘石市看守所；一个月后，又被以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被吉林省盘石市法院宣布重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，经二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。目前在吉林省长春市宽城区兴业监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">敬慧玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川南充市南部县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，家住四川南充市南部县，原南部县农行职工。一九九六年，她开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午，在公交车上，敬慧玲给几个学生讲法轮功被迫害的真相，被南部县国保大队副大队长蒙长军等人抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，南部县法院两次对她庭审，均因证据不当而无果。敬慧玲曾质问：到底哪条法律因我发了两个<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，打了几个电话，就被破坏了法律？即使这样，敬慧玲仍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后她被转至成都女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">荆建秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑州市法轮功学员。女，六十多岁，家住河南郑州市上街区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，周喜云在荆建秋家中做客，她俩一起被荥阳广武派出所警察、荥阳国保大队警察抓捕，被关押在郑州第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在中原区法院南办公区被开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，荆建秋和周喜云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">鞠殿红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鞠世淼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，辽宁凤城法轮功学员，原辽宁省直信息总台财务人员。为修炼法轮功，鞠世淼曾多次去北京上访，曾被拘留，劳教，合计<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，丹东市凤城市法轮功学员鞠世淼、孙忠琴、佟秀红，在凤城大兴镇，给村民送明慧新年台历、福字和期刊等，被大兴镇政法综治委员宋传刚等人抓捕，后被构陷到丹东市振安区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被丹东市振安区法院判刑：鞠世淼被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；孙忠琴<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；佟秀红<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。佟秀红于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被“取保候审”，已回家。鞠世淼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">K</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卡地尔丁<span lang="EN-US">. </span>吐达訇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卡姆巴尔•阿穆巴尔大毛拉（维吾尔族）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">康启惠、康卓才丹（藏）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">克尤木•穆罕默德（维）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肯杰别克﹒阿纳尔别克（哈萨克）、肯杰别克•达列力（哈萨克）、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孔令坡、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孔文涛、寇爱梅、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邝德英、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卡地尔丁<span lang="EN-US">. </span>吐达訇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆维吾尔自治区克拉玛依市维吾尔族青年，天津商业大学的在校学生，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年暑假假期回家就再也没有能返回学校。今获悉他已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被克拉玛依市公安局以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨罪、民族歧视罪正式逮捕。目前羁押于克拉玛依市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">卡姆巴尔<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿穆巴尔大毛拉（维吾尔族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆和田市哈尼埃里克镇人，维族名<span lang="EN-US">Qamber Amber Damolla</span>，新疆维吾尔族著名宗教学者，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在新疆和田市哈尼埃里克镇高中曾有<span lang="EN-US">17</span>名维吾尔族人被中共和田市当局抓捕，指控他们的言行涉及了与国家安全有关的各种罪名，卡姆巴尔<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿穆巴尔大毛拉亦是其中之一。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获悉，其终因不与中共新疆当局合作，而被新疆和田市中级法院以“危害国家安全罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">康启惠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，安徽省合肥市肥东县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日向民众宣讲法轮功遭抓捕、构陷，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半、罚金八千元。康启惠上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日二审没有开庭，维持冤判，随后康启惠被劫持到安徽女子监狱迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">康卓才丹（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海省黄南藏族自治州泽库县多禾茂乡多禾日村人，藏族词曲创作人，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因参与了<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年青海省黄南州藏人学生的“挺藏语”示威游行活动，随被黄南州泽库县警方予以拘捕，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月才被获释；之后其虽被准予获释返家，但因当局恐其再次组织、参与学生抗议活动，遂对其仍进行严密监控，截至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，其身份证件均被没收，欲返回学校亦被禁止，且其在社会上的所有活动都几乎被限；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，又因创作了一首颂扬西藏精神领袖达赖喇嘛的歌曲，并由当地歌手才果广为演唱，之后其两人即遭黄南州泽库县警方抓捕、刑拘；后很快被当地泽库县检察院以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家”等罪予以批捕，并被关押于泽库县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，其案在青海省黄南州泽库县法院进行庭审，终被一审以“煽动分裂国家罪” 、“对外泄露国家机密罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。目前疑似在黄南藏族自治州泽库县监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">克尤木•穆罕默德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族，又被译为克尤木<span lang="EN-US">.</span>买买提，新疆艺术学院副教授，影视演员，主持人，维吾尔表演艺术家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">早年情况不详，只知其曾因长期在新疆乌鲁木齐市的新疆艺术学院担任副教授，且担任维吾尔青年演员的导师，故而深受维吾尔族裔师生及社会各界人士喜爱、尊敬和推崇；曾被业界及社会大众誉为维吾尔青年表演艺术家和喜剧演员的“表演大师”；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其突然从舞台、论坛及表演场馆等消失，自此无其任何讯息；后在国际维吾尔人权与民主基金会的不断追踪和查寻下，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日获悉，其被新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市警方以不具名罪由已经秘密拘押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多；据悉，其在密押期间，一直在被调查中，至今未审不放。目前被羁押地点不明。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_27.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3_27.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">肯杰别克﹒阿纳尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年龄不详，新疆博乐市人，哈萨克族，异见人士。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，因其从哈萨克斯坦国探亲回国后，在微信群里转发了一些移民哈萨克斯坦国的信息，发表了相关言论，并协助本村村民移民哈萨克斯坦国，被当地警方知晓，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被新疆博乐市警方以</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">​​​​</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出卖国家机密罪”为罪由拘捕，之后一直失联；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被新疆维吾尔自治区博乐市法院一审以“泄露国家秘密罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前被关押于新疆博乐市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肯杰别克•达列力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孔令坡：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东曲阜市后彭村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日中午，孔令坡在曲阜市董庄镇发放法轮功资料时，被曲阜市董庄派出所抓捕。当天孔令坡被抄家，抄走了家中的大法书籍、视频机、音频机、光盘和和几十元零钱，还抢走了孔令坡的手机，并把孔令坡的妻子抓捕到小雪镇派出所。当天，他妻子被送回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孔令坡被拘留，被关押在泗水县拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，没有通知家人，家人曾多次问询无果。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孔文涛，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">66</span>年生，江苏南京人，副主任医师，南京高淳区人民医院消化内科主任，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年毕业于南京医学院，堪称南京本地的名流望族。因追求民主宪政，期望建立一个法治国家，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初被当局逮捕，今天有消息传来，孔文涛被以颠覆国家政权罪判刑十三年，当庭认罪，且不上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">寇爱梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陕西宝鸡石油机械厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宝鸡市金台公安分局出动了多辆警车、几十个警察，抓捕了宝鸡石油机械厂的八名法轮功学员及家属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，秦丽杰、李宝莲、寇爱梅三人被关押到宝鸡第二看守所非法逮捕、关押，其他人已于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被释放回家。后获悉秦丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，寇爱梅被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，李宝莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。寇爱梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邝德英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。邝德英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日<span lang="EN-US">13</span>时许，在昆明市西山区海口镇粘土矿出租房内被敲门进来的警察搜查，抢劫了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>些法轮功书籍刊物等，被关押到派出所盘问调查。后被刑事拘留、逮捕<span lang="EN-US">/</span>起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午，邝德英被西山法院第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次视频开庭；判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
